944:\\\\n  > 945:    This function is a deterministic fallback ensuring ``_determine_phase_status()``\\\\n  > 946:    always finds a valid result file for phases that exit 0 but write no report.\\\\n  > 947:    Without it, such phases return ``PASS_NO_REPORT`` because no result file is present.\\\\n  > 948:\\\\n  > 949:    **Ordering invariant**: Call *after* ``finished_at`` is captured and If called after status determination,\\\\n  > 951:    the sentinel file will not affect the already-computed status.\\\\n  > 952:\\\\n  > 953:    **Concurrency**: Assumes single-threaded execution (one phase at a time). If the\\\\n  > 954:    sprint loop is parallelised in future, this function must be replaced with an\\\\n  > 955:    ``O_EXCL``-based atomic write to prevent TOCTOU races between the exists-check\\\\n  > 956:    and the write.\\\\n  > 957:\\\\n  > 958:    **Sentinel contract**: Writes ``EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n`` so that\\\\n  > 959:    ``_determine_phase_status()`` branch 3 (``result_file.exists()`` → CONTINUE check\\\\n  > 960:    at line 1024) returns ``PhaseStatus.PASS`` instead of falling through to the\\\\n  > 961:    ``PASS_NO_REPORT`` branch (line 1045).
